          SELECT TOP(1) [e].[Id], [e].[Contato], [e].[Datacadastro], [e].[Descricaoevento], [e].[Email], [e].[Imagempersonalida], [e].[Instituicao], [e].[Linksparainscricao], [e].[Nomecompleto], [e].[Numeroparticipantes], [e].[Publicaosite], [e].[Status], [e].[Subtitulo], [e].[Tipoevento], [e].[Titulo]
          FROM [EventosSebraeLab] AS [e]
          WHERE [e].[Id] = @__id_0
      ) AS [t]
      LEFT JOIN [DiasEventoSebraeLab] AS [d] ON [t].[Id] = [d].[Eventoid]
      ORDER BY [t].[Id]
